							round_temp_variable = MLW_steel_produced

				}
				option = { # FOSSIL FUEL OPTION - 1 YEAR
					trigger = { has_country_flag = MLW_fossil_fuel_option }
					name = MLW_UDF.90.O2
					log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MLW_UDF.90.O2 executed"
					259 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = fuel_silo
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = fossil_powerplant
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
					260 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = fossil_powerplant
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = fuel_silo
							level = 2
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.3 }
					update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
					clr_country_flag = MLW_fossil_fuel_option
				}
				option = { # GREEN ENERGY OPTION - 2 YEARS
					trigger = { has_country_flag = MLW_green_energy_option }
					name = MLW_UDF.90.O3
					log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MLW_UDF.90.O3 executed"
					260 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = offices
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
						add_building_construction = {
							type = synthetic_refinery
							level = 2
							instant_build = yes
						}
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					}
					set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.3 }
					update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
					clr_country_flag = MLW_green_energy_option
				}
			}
		# YOUTH BUSINESS GRANT EVENTS - 11
			country_event = {
				id = MLW_UDF.11
				title = MLW_UDF.11.t
				desc = MLW_UDF.11.d
				#picture = ADD
				is_triggered_only = yes
				immediate = {
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { MLW_youth_grants_given < 3 } }
						country_event = {
							id = MLW_UDF.11
							days = 360
						}
					}
				}
				option = {
					name = MLW_UDF.11.O1
					log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MLW_UDF.11.O1 executed"
					random_list = {
						70 = {
							set_temp_variable = { DM_bureau_cost_change = -0.075 }
							update_MLW_UDF_centralisation_cost = yes
						}
						30 = {
							random_list = {
								70 = {
									random_owned_state = {
										add_building_construction = {
											type = industrial_complex
											level = 1
											instant_build = yes
										}
										add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
									}
								}
								30 = {
									random_owned_state = {
										add_building_construction = {
											type = offices
											level = 1
											instant_build = yes
										}
										add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
									}
								}
							}
							set_temp_variable = { DM_bureau_cost_change = -0.075 }
							update_MLW_UDF_centralisation_cost = yes
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { MLW_youth_grants_given = 1 }
				}
			}
		# FISHERY AID ENDS - 12
			country_event = {
				id = MLW_UDF.12
				title = MLW_UDF.12.t
				desc = MLW_UDF.12.d
				#picture = ADD
				is_triggered_only = yes
				option = {
					name = MLW_UDF.12.O1
					log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MLW_UDF.12.O1 executed"
					if = {
						limit = { has_completed_focus = MLW_utilize_oil }
						set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = MLW_stored_fishing_income }
						multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = 1.5 }
						update_MLW_UDF_policies_income = yes
						clear_variable = MLW_stored_fishing_income
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_owns_no_lake_states = yes }
							set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = gdp_total }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.01 }
							update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
						}
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_owns_one_lake_state = yes }
							set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = gdp_total }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.01 }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = 1.25 }
							update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
						}
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_owns_two_lake_states = yes }
							set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = gdp_total }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.01 }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = 1.5 }
							update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
						}
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_owns_all_lake_states = yes }
							set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = gdp_total }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.01 }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = 1.75 }
							update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
						}
					}
					# for no oil exploitation
					if = {
						limit = { has_completed_focus = MLW_avoid_backlash }
						set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = MLW_stored_fishing_income }
						multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = 3 }
						update_MLW_UDF_policies_income = yes
						clear_variable = MLW_stored_fishing_income
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_owns_no_lake_states = yes }
							set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = gdp_total }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.005 }
							update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
						}
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_owns_one_lake_state = yes }
							set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = gdp_total }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.005 }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = 1.25 }
							update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
						}
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_owns_two_lake_states = yes }
							set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = gdp_total }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.005 }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = 1.5 }
							update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
						}
						if = {
							limit = { MLW_owns_all_lake_states = yes }
							set_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = gdp_total }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = -0.005 }
							multiply_temp_variable = { DM_additional_money_change = 1.75 }
							update_MLW_UDF_policies_expenses = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}

# NEWS EVENTS
news_event = {
	id = MLW_MZ_major.1
	title = MLW_MZ_major.1.t
	desc = MLW_MZ_major.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	option = { # I THOUGHT DECOLONISATION ENDED?
		name = MLW_MZ_major.1.O1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = ENG
					original_tag = MLW
					original_tag = STH
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # JOLLY GOOD BIT OF BUSINESS THAT
		name = MLW_MZ_major.1.O2
		trigger = { original_tag = ENG }
	}
	option = { # A NEW SEZ FOR OUR OPERATIONS
		name = MLW_MZ_major.1.O3
		trigger = { original_tag = MLW }
	}
	option = { # WE LOOK FORWARDS TO THE FUTURE!
		name = MLW_MZ_major.1.O4
		trigger = { original_tag = STH }
	}
